new entry "RIFT_STRIKE"
type "StatusData"
data "StatusType" "BOOST"
data "Boosts" "IF(IsWeaponOfProficiencyGroup('Battleaxes|Clubs|Daggers|Flails|Glaives|Greataxes|Greatclubs|Greatswords|Halberds|Handaxes|Javelins|LightHammers|Longswords|Maces|Mauls|Morningstars|Pikes|Quarterstaffs|Rapiers|Scimitars|Shortswords|Sickles|Spears|Tridents|Warhammers|Warpicks', GetActiveWeapon())):UnlockSpell(Target_RiftStrike);IF(IsWeaponOfProficiencyGroup('Darts|HandCrossbows|HeavyCrossbows|LightCrossbows|Longbows|Shortbows|Slings', GetActiveWeapon())):UnlockSpell(Projectile_RiftStrike)"
data "RemoveConditions" "SpellId('Target_RiftStrike') or SpellId('Projectile_RiftStrike')"
data "RemoveEvents" "OnSpellCast"
data "TickType" "EndTurn"
data "StatusPropertyFlags" "DisableCombatlog;DisablePortraitIndicator;DisableOverhead"

new entry "PHASE_SLASH_TARGET"
type "StatusData"
data "StatusType" "BOOST"
data "StatusPropertyFlags" "DisableCombatlog;DisablePortraitIndicator;DisableOverhead"
